button-containerobFfV0vf6giV"><div id="content-head"><h1 class="Title Title1 ai-heading-padding1LUkZsE3r9To">Comment display name</h1></div></div></header><div class="rm-Markdown markdown-body content-body" data-testid="RDMD"><p>The Comment Display Name object represents the author name that shows up for a comment. This overrides the default author name when specified.</p>
<h2 class="heading heading-2 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="request-format-input"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-request-format-input" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Request format (input)</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Request format (input)" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#request-format-input"></a></h2>
<h3 class="heading heading-3 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="object-properties"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-object-properties" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Object properties</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Object properties" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#object-properties"></a></h3>























<div class="rdmd-table"><div class="rdmd-table-inner"><table><thead><tr><th style="text-align:left">Parameter</th><th style="text-align:left">Type</th><th style="text-align:left">Description</th><th style="text-align:left">Example value</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td style="text-align:left"><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">type</code></td><td style="text-align:left"><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">string</code><br/>
(enum)</td><td style="text-align:left">Possible type values are:<button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">&quot;integration&quot;</code>, <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">&quot;user&quot;</code>, or <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">&quot;custom&quot;</code></td><td style="text-align:left"><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">&quot;user&quot;</code></td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:left"><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">custom</code></td><td style="text-align:left"><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">object</code></td><td style="text-align:left">If the type is <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">&quot;custom&quot;</code>, include a custom object specifying the custom name<br/><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">&quot;custom&quot;: {      &quot;name&quot;: &lt;Custom Name&gt;	 }</code></td><td style="text-align:left"><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">&quot;custom&quot;: {    &quot;name&quot;: &quot;Notion Bot&quot;	 }</code></td></tr></tbody></table></div></div>
<ul>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">&quot;integration&quot;</code>: name of the <a target="_self" href="/docs/getting-started">integration</a></li>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">&quot;user&quot;</code>: name of the user who authenticated the integration (only for <a target="_self" href="/docs/getting-started#internal-vs-public-integrations">Public Integrations</a>)</li>
<li><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">&quot;custom&quot;</code>: any custom name</li>
</ul>
<p>Example of a Create Comment request with custom display name:</p>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">API request</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-json theme-light" data-lang="json" name="API request" tabindex="0">{
  &quot;parent&quot;: {
    &quot;page_id&quot;: &quot;d0a1ffaf-a4d8-4acf-a1ed-abae6e110418&quot;
  },
  &quot;rich_text&quot;: [
    {
      &quot;text&quot;: {
        &quot;content&quot;: &quot;Thanks for checking us out!&quot;
      }
    }
  ],
  &quot;display_name&quot;: {
    &quot;type&quot;: &quot;custom&quot;,
    &quot;custom&quot;: {
      &quot;name&quot;: &quot;Notion Bot&quot;
    }
  }
}
</code></pre></div></div>
<h2 class="heading heading-2 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="response-format-output"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-response-format-output" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Response format (output)</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Response format (output)" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#response-format-output"></a></h2>
<h3 class="heading heading-3 header-scroll" align=""><div class="heading-anchor anchor waypoint" id="object-properties-1"></div><div class="heading-text"><div id="section-object-properties" class="heading-anchor_backwardsCompatibility"></div>Object properties</div><a aria-label="Skip link to Object properties" class="heading-anchor-icon fa fa-anchor" href="#object-properties-1"></a></h3>
<p>The response of Comment APIs like <a target="_self" href="/reference/create-a-comment">Create comment</a> contains <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">attachments</code> with the following fields:</p>























<div class="rdmd-table"><div class="rdmd-table-inner"><table><thead><tr><th style="text-align:left">Field</th><th style="text-align:left">Type</th><th style="text-align:left">Description</th><th style="text-align:left">Example value</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td style="text-align:left"><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">type</code></td><td style="text-align:left"><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">string</code> (enum)</td><td style="text-align:left">Possible type values are:<button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">&quot;integration&quot;</code>, <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">&quot;user&quot;</code>, or <button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">&quot;custom&quot;</code></td><td style="text-align:left"><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">&quot;custom&quot;</code></td></tr><tr><td style="text-align:left"><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">resolved_name</code></td><td style="text-align:left"><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">string</code></td><td style="text-align:left">The custom display name shown in a comment</td><td style="text-align:left"><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang- theme-light" data-lang="" name="" tabindex="0">&quot;Notion Bot&quot;</code></td></tr></tbody></table></div></div>
<br/>
<div class="CodeTabs CodeTabs_initial theme-light"><div class="CodeTabs-toolbar" role="tablist"><button aria-selected="true" class="CodeTabs_active" role="tab" type="button">API Response</button></div><div class="CodeTabs-inner" role="tabpanel"><pre><button aria-label="Copy Code" class="rdmd-code-copy fa"></button><code class="rdmd-code lang-json theme-light" data-lang="json" name="API Response" tabindex="0">{
  ...existing parameters omitted,
  &quot;display_name&quot;: {
    &quot;type&quot;: &quot;custom&quot;,
    &quot;resolved_name&quot;: &quot;Notion Bot&quot;
  }
}
</code></pre></div></div></div></article><section class="content-toc grid-25"><nav><ul class="toc-list"><li><a class="tocHeader" href="#"><i class="icon icon-text-align-left"></i>Table of Contents</a></li><li class="toc-children"><ul>

Comment Display Name object represents the author name that shows up for a comment. This overrides the default author name when specified.\n\n## Request format (input)\n\n### Object properties\n\n[block:parameters]\n{\n  \&quot;data\&quot;: {\n    \&quot;h-0\&quot;: \&quot;Parameter\&quot;,\n    \&quot;h-1\&quot;: \&quot;Type\&quot;,\n    \&quot;h-2\&quot;: \&quot;Description\&quot;,\n    \&quot;h-3\&quot;: \&quot;Example value\&quot;,\n    \&quot;0-0\&quot;: \&quot;`type`\&quot;,\n    \&quot;0-1\&quot;: \&quot;`string`  \\n(enum)\&quot;,\n    \&quot;0-2\&quot;: \&quot;Possible type values are:`\\\&quot;integration\\\&quot;`, `\\\&quot;user\\\&quot;`, or `\\\&quot;custom\\\&quot;`\&quot;,\n    \&quot;0-3\&quot;: \&quot;`\\\&quot;user\\\&quot;`\&quot;,\n    \&quot;1-0\&quot;: \&quot;`custom`\&quot;,\n    \&quot;1-1\&quot;: \&quot;`object`\&quot;,\n    \&quot;1-2\&quot;: \&quot;If the type is `\\\&quot;custom\\\&quot;`, include a custom object specifying the custom name  \\n`\\\&quot;custom\\\&quot;: {  \\n   \\\&quot;name\\\&quot;: &lt;Custom Name&gt;\\t\\n}`\&quot;,\n    \&quot;1-3\&quot;: \&quot;`\\\&quot;custom\\\&quot;: {\\n   \\\&quot;name\\\&quot;: \\\&quot;Notion Bot\\\&quot;\\t\\n}`\&quot;\n  },\n  \&quot;cols\&quot;: 4,\n  \&quot;rows\&quot;: 2,\n  \&quot;align\&quot;: [\n    \&quot;left\&quot;,\n    \&quot;left\&quot;,\n    \&quot;left\&quot;,\n    \&quot;left\&quot;\n  ]\n}\n[/block]\n\n\n- `\&quot;integration\&quot;`: name of the [integration](doc:getting-started)\n- `\&quot;user\&quot;`: name of the user who authenticated the integration (only for [Public Integrations](https://developers.notion.com/docs/getting-started#internal-vs-public-integrations))\n- `\&quot;custom\&quot;`: any custom name\n\nExample of a Create Comment request with custom display name:\n\n```json API request\n{\n  \&quot;parent\&quot;: {\n    \&quot;page_id\&quot;: \&quot;d0a1ffaf-a4d8-4acf-a1ed-abae6e110418\&quot;\n  },\n  \&quot;rich_text\&quot;: [\n    {\n   \&quot;custom\&quot;: {\n      \&quot;name\&quot;: \&quot;Notion Bot\&quot;\n    }\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Response format (output)\n\n### Object properties\n\nThe response of Comment APIs like [Create
